Abstract\n\nThe aerodynamic design and analysis of three blended wing-fuselage\nsupersonic cruise configurations\nproviding four-, five-,\nand six-abreast\nseating\nhas been conducted using a previously designed supersonic cruise configuration\nas the baseline.\nThe five-abreast\nconfiguration\nwas optimized for wave drag at\na Mach number of 2.7.\nThe four- and six-abreast\nconfigurations\nwere also optimized at Mach 2.7, but with the added constraint\nthat the majority\nof their\nstructure\nbe commonwith the five-abreast\nconfiguration.\nAnalysis of the three\nconfigurations\nindicated an improvement of 6.0, 7.5, and 7.7 percent in cruise\nlift-to-drag\nratio over the baseline configuration\nfor the four-, five-,\nand\nsix-abreast\nconfigurations,\nrespectively.\nValidation\nof the design is planned\nthrough supersonic wind tunnel tests.\n\n17.
